<Z>Gridstats Retro and New Startups <C> It's been an interesting couple of weeks. Having been unsure about sending out a free <L.31.1>
offer a couple of weekends ago, we've had over fifty take-ups. That offer is still open (see below) but it's also led to me <L.31.1>
launching Gridstats Retro. This has now set up, but if you want to join a standby waiting list let me know.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Free Startups <C> I'm still running the offer of a free startup (first two turns) in any of the games currently running (Play On, <L.31.1>
Gridstats and Soccer Stats are all suspended), though see above for Gridstats Retro for any new players, returning players or <L.31.1>
existing players who want to try their hand at a new game. The rationale is simple, it's straightforward for me to do, there's a <L.31.1>
fair chance some folk out there might be looking to pick up an old game, and yes, somewhere down the line you may have to pay for <L.31.1>
the turns, though that's far from the driving force. If you fancy taking up a new team, or reviving your existing one, drop me an <L.31.1>
email. Feel free to flag up these games to friends and family - the more the merrier when people have time on their hands.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Games and Coronovirus <C> Obviously the new few months are going to be somewhat different for society than we're used to, but as <L.31.1>
far as running games are concerned, the plan is to go ahead as normal. Other games, not dependent on real life results will go <L.31.1>
ahead. I'll keep the latest news of www.pbmsports.com up to date, including when games have been run, so please check there first. <L.31.1>
If it doesn't say they've been run, they've not been run, and that may mean I'm focussed on "other stuff" (health or family <L.31.1>
health) so please do check there first. Best wishes to everyone, be sensible and keep safe over the coming months.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Late Turns <C> Deadlines are 9am Saturday. Please assume weekend turns will be run either Saturday or Sunday (i.e. please<L.31.1>
don't chase me up Sunday for "missing turns"). I run these games in my spare time, so the more efficient that is the better. <L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Playing Online/Postage Costs <C> Note that from the start of April, I'm now considering all games to be "online first", and<L.31.1>
if you do want/need a posted copy of the results, there's an extra 0.4 credit charge. Please try and use email if possible<L.31.1>
